--- Commit Message ---
LU-13805 llite: Implement unaligned DIO connect flag

Unupgraded ZFS servers may crash if they received unaligned
DIO, so we need a compat flag and a test to recognize those
servers.

This patch implements that logic.

Fixes: 7194eb6431 ("LU-13805 clio: bounce buffer for unaligned DIO")
Signed-off-by: Patrick Farrell <pfarrell@whamcloud.com>

Patch Set 40: Code-Review-1

(8 comments)

I recall we discussed this, but I'm not totally onboard with the implementation. I think it could be more isolated and not depend on exposing and checking the FSTYPE for every write. 

The same could be had by always *setting* the UNALIGNED_DIO flag for ldiskfs (small maxbytes) servers after connection. That can be version limited on the client (eg. before 2.19.53) and also backport the setting of this flag for ldiskfs servers, and after that we assume the servers are exposing this flag correctly.
